\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
Interprets the scan codes from the keyboard for the EN\+\_\+\+US keyboard layout. 

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{keyboard_8h_source_l00295}{295}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{keyboard_8h_source}{keyboard.\+h}}.
